Dhandhanggula

Edited by Kartika Setyawati

  • Witness
  • Metadata

Description of the witness

  • Manuscript Identity:
    • Settlement: Leiden
    • Institution: University Library (UB)
    • Repository: Lontar
    • Identifier: Or. 23732
  • Work: Vipañcitārthā by Śāntarakṣita
  • Physical Description:
    • History: In June 1934, Sāṅkṛtyāyana found this manuscript in the monastery of Kun-de-ling (Lhasa).

    Metadata of the Edition

    • Title: Dhandhanggula.
    • Text Identifier: DHARMA_DiplEd_F
    • Edited by Kartika Setyawati
    • Copyright © 2019-2025 by Kartika Setyawati.

    This project has received funding from the European Research Council (ERC) under the European Union's Horizon 2020 research and innovation programme (grant agreement no 809994).

    .


    Folio 1rDhandhanggula /0// oṃ awig̈na nama śidḍi //0//

    1.

    apasaṅ tabe kamw amariñci hamijilakĕn tatwani smara, ḍa/puriṅ śabda kaṅ pinet muḍa tan wri riṅ laku raga milw aƞikĕt karasmin sampun tan iƞapura deniṅ saṅ tameṅ wruḥ kuma.... sa/met raras kumaliƞa hanilad. wijiliṅ sandi tilasiṅra saṅ wusman.
    ø hanut ri raśanira sanira saƞ adi ḍa/ḍaṅgula tĕmbaṅniṅ wacana, pupuḥ tirwan ta riṅƞ amet mahaṙdḍikaniṅ tĕmbaṅ panalimuṙ mendraniṅ budi raga ka gĕṅ kaḷƞĕƞan. wuṙ/yya manaḥ jinum. syuḥ śiṙnanniṅ cipta ƞambara, pinagatanitwasaṅ rusit saṅ nalemoṙr iṅ driya
    ø juwama nut ṣwa/raniṅ sukmalit pan amun. cipta daṙpa śuk.skaṙ, dibwa wahu saṅ kamuṙkana mĕwĕ duta malulut kiraṅ yog̈a pramada lwiḥ/ winoteṅ kanuragan. jñana śalaṅ śurup., daṙsana traś.na niṅtyaśa tan kagiwaṅ śumĕṅ pamacanani śaḥ dyaniṅƞ a/mriḥ carita
    ø nahan saṅsiptaniƞ amarici saṅƞ amagiḥ tusṭa moṅ kawiṙyyan riṅ wilatikna pranaḥhe pralabda prabu wibuḥ watĕk da
    Folio 1vna mule kaśwesiḥ     hasikĕp kasusilan. pramaṙta budy alus pinampu śakala, kasub kaṛƞĕ hapunya hadana lawiḥ/- boga sadana lumraḥ
    ø tlas deniraƞ amukti karasmin winusana saṅƞ atitaḥ mapann atuwa wayahe, tutug. wṛtiniṅ tuwuḥ/ luwaṙ tanṣaḥ mukti sumilib. śamaya magiḥ prana mitanira luarut., pramana śukmaniṅ raga sinakitan tig̈aṅ di/na lawasniki hanahurakĕn. pjaḥ
    ø hatigal tanayestri kakaliḥ lanaṅ tuƞgal. hapadudyan maṙga putra gana wikan i/ reḥ, saṅ yayaḥ tibra lampus. hamupuśi pura sumiwi śu laha piniraṅ lagwanom tan. wriṅ hyun tan sinuƞan ra/ja yogwa kasihanitwasa kuṅ mapan rare halit dalu tanpa puhara
    ø śatatwa laraniṅ daya, rarwanom haja ƞuni/ƞuniƞa, yena krama śapa wogan iku tĕmbe yaktiku hamulaƞuni kumara yayaḥ, hapanas titahakna make śa/deniṅ ƞadu matikaḥ kṛptiniṅ jñana haguṅṛnan hana make ki śiƞamada halitan. wri reḥ, sanake nora na .....
    Folio 2r di     mapan tuƞgal. yayaḥ maṙmane pa tanpa mule
    ø wuwusĕn ki siƞamada kari katigal. pjaḥ wwaṙniṅ bapa nastapa ha/puwara ƞe yayaḥ bu dibra lampus kawlas aṙśa duka priyatin ramestri tumut abela, kari tanpa nuśu saṅsara ƞmaśi la/ra kanastapā hanaƞi rahina wƞi yayebu makasabat
    ø kakaṅ histri kakaliḥ hamukti kapal sami denira śaṅ/ śuka maƞki tan ketaṅƞ arine, ki śiƞamada lusuḥ śiṅ wwaṅ śudi hamilaśani śaya tuwa ri wayaḥ saṅsipta riṅ laku, nisṭaniṅ/ raga karaśa winiweka duka nastapane lwiḥ śwaraśaniṅ wṛdaya
    ø kadi rag̈ane tan ana sudi śiƞamada śina/guḥ hapana mulane nisṭa riṅ deśa, saparaniṅ laku la luƞa haƞikis lampus tan pamit., luƞa śakiṅ pradeśa lampas lapa/ḥhipun. riṅ wanapriga kahaṙśa riṅ duṙggamā ḃaya kewĕ wwaṙ tan kahiṣti dahat gĕṅniṅ kalaran.
    ø śaya lapas lampaḥhira ta/n ana katoliḥ cipta laƞut lampus niṅ katṛśnan., hanĕśĕl. raganipun ṣuka pjaḥ hawane saṅsayaniṅ rag̈a tan sipi tan wruḥ ri rama rena, na...tapa huwuhu/wu harahaƞiṅ kawasa paƞeran. mon kagugu kagoraweṅ twĕs asiƞit. raga tan wruḥ ƞenak.
    ø kuna yen ana kĕsĕliƞ ati baya luhuṅ haƞuṅsi/ya waṇa sṛmma nusapa ƞoṅ maṅke pjaḥha luhuṙ gunuṅ yen mijila wacaṇa niki, winiweka riṅ nala rumumpa woṅƞ ayu, datan kawaṙṇnaheṅ maṙga tlas. lari/s. lampaḥnya hasaƞu taƞiṣ prapta jĕṅ ni prawata
    ø hamagiḥ ḍukuḥ welahaṙja mikiṅƞakĕn maṙgga mulat ki siƞamada sakṣana reren jĕṅ rapuḥ cipta/ pa ƞliḥ kapagiḥ saṅ tapa ligiḥ ri mada sambrama ki paƞuwusan haligiḥya paƞeran ṣa tami ḍataṅ mara ke hañaṙ wikan. ƞoṅ kaki, lwiṙ tan. sṙṅ priya/... polaḥe laḥ bapa hamaratiya wri naya ki siƞamada sami haligiḥ ki habit. liṅnya tatakon. di sakan taku kaki sumahu/r alon. mawa/raḥ pikane
    ø tuhu tan. wikan. wartin. ta kaki ƞoṅ bapa tanya swapa naman.ta waraḥ jati kami make siƞamada wriṅ smu saṅ tabe namaya
    Folio 3r ranakta kaki     hapajara ri nama, manawi tuhhu tan wruḥ siƞamaḋa haraniṅ waṅ ḋahat deniṅ hamukti nastapa lwiḥ kawlas aṙsa sityasa
    ø aƞusi kaḋaṅ wṛga tan ṣudi tuu/ dinaliḥ tik.na/ wiruda ḋata øa sudi kabeḥ pjaḥ pa rama hibu karakasa ƞg n i kari ki habĕt mawacaṇana ƞṛs. twaskw aruƞu samono denta wacana ki paƞuwusa/n aƞliṅ haƞṛs ta wisṭi ki baru maṅraṅkeya
    ø saṅ ṣikṣya prapta wot.skaṙ punapi kaṙyya ƞawe sya dan pala boga ..enpunasereg ṣa tami hasmu ƞliḥ tan lagana ki ḃaru/ mintaṙ laky age hagli... lampaḥhiƞ utusan. mdal punaṅ pupuḍutan. skul ...hiḍan kalan bitutu tetep laḥ ta byakṣa sa tami tuwuḥ sampun bapa denira pu/puḍen.
    ø tan. wuwusĕn. denya byakṣa prapti haṙtali mugwiṅ talika, maḍaṅ samya wusan tan asuwe hyaṅƞ aṙka myaṅ kasumurup. wulan saṅ tapa haṅliṅ denpun./ṣateśe manaḥ sunya nikaṅ ḍukuḥ siƞamaḋa mawacana hantyanta pan akaṙyya dibya matitis. tuhu myaṅtwani jiwa
    ø ƞ kapiluḥ swaranira ki wasi tan ṣipi maṙ/mmanira tumiƞal haƞṛs. raṣane hatine mulat. waṙnaniṅ tamu ya ḍuḥ eman tan ana kṛti naya solaḥ jatmika rupane habagus. punapa saṅkane/ luƞa pasewaka/ priḥ rag̈anira nak mamaṙ ma.. ..maṅgiḥ lara
    ø siƞamadya hanampani wisṭi wikan parinayaniṅ wacana, śumarapratwaseṅ rate/ pasaṅ surudi laku tan katoliḥ rasminiṅ ganti, kdĕniṅ cipta brata, ƞoṅwaḥhana laku sawisayanikiṅ mala, naƞi ketuṅ pra/sidahaniƞ akikin. weniṅ rag̈a nastapa
    ø melik tan aṙṣa kuraṅƞ amukti riṅƞ aśewaka hakweḥ bayanya, hamĕwĕ/ lara guƞe sira saṅ janma lawu paratinḍā mewĕ haruci ranak hyaṅ tan. wri naya, hakol piḍa puguṅ, tan kage śola śwara/ tanpa sanḍaṅ hakumul. tuṙ kumalikiḥ haṅlud tanpa sadana
    ø waniḥ saṅƞ asewakaha hamriḥ kitri habrakane śuka sugi/ḥya, ha maṙggane hamosel. tapuwara hanugu pulakṛti kaṅ denulatti hapaksa ƞadu titaḥ laba denpalaku ha
    Folio 4rƞi masa katkana,     haṅraƞkal. wisayane kagiri giri kaƞelann amet ṣuka
    ø maṙmmane raga ƞuśi waṇnadri ha/ƞowahanā gĕṅniṅ wisaya, haja dene kadi make lara lapa katĕmu, śagonane sarira hiki nisṭa yen sampun ti/ƞkaḥ wus dum wawakisun sandeniṅƞ aṛp.lwiha, rag̈a nisṭa kapuraṅ tann apawṛti haƞel. yen ulatana
    ø gantaṅ/ hupamanipun. kĕḷm hana riṅ samudra masa li ta tawata hisine, pan. wus takĕripun hamĕwĕƞhi lara kaseśiḥ ma/ toniṅ niṅƞ asuka niṅƞ amukti rame, tan apik. prana hilaƞa riṅ gunuṅ riṅƞ ampaḥ pasnĕtane hawrat kalabane ha/ƞahub. śwaṙriṅ piśiś nisṭa dama tan ana pulakṛtinipun.
    ø pacĕ wṛdayanira hyaṅ waśi hamihaṙsa pasraṅniṅ wacana, hano/m. pratama hujare da kaśilib ciptaniṅsun. halaḥ dene raronwam. kawi lampus tan. tṛsne śarat. hapaksa/ ṛ pkap laku dibwa malaṙ tape wana, śramma kahanaśira saṅ tapa śakti biksuka maƞan ṣukla
    ø patwa waṣa ƞoṅ kaki haƞalaƞi
    Folio 4v pratikaḥhira mahaśewana,     riṅ sun apinḍa tan pawe, mewĕ bapa riṅ laku lagwa wayaḥ kita nak mami riṅƞ aƞuśwakĕ/n. brata, kweḥ bacananipun panalibniṅ daśendriya, tapaśenaku bapa riṅƞ aƞawaśi paƞuwusan iṅ yoga
    ø sawaƞn/ riṅ sun iṅ lampa kaki śarira tan. kneṅ ƞaku juga, wastunĕn makin asuwe tan parimana hewuh duṙggamaƞel maṙgani kitri/ tan.n oliḥ imaniman pira saṅ kṛtayu, tan kasalanan wig̈raha tiwas bisā lakw ayu tan. kneṅƞ isṭi harok lumaksanaha/
    ø śiƞamada hanakiṅsun kaki wṛdi hati waspada ƞucap. wruḥ riṅ laku sabda mule, haƞiṅ dipuntumulus. kawasa/ha raganta kaki praḥ śwara kaṅƞ utama, ḍuḥ sawƞn riṅ pun gĕṅniṅ tṛsna humori ṅ rag̈a, tanakna pinuraṅ saṅƞ atapa sakti sampun kṛtiśa/maya
    ø madyaniṅ ratri kahaṙsa ki paƞabĕt lagwa wacana, mapitutuṙ prayoganiṅ lakw aƞne siƞamada nampani kawĕ/ƞan ciptanira winaraḥ riṅ reḥ hayo ta kitā kabakaba lkasi tapa mudita dipunawas. glariṅ laku kaṅ pinet. niṙ lka
    Folio 5rsniṅ wirati danapunya yen tan. wruḥ panuga     tanda talinglane
    ø waneḥ bapa natariṅƞ akikin hakwe bawā lkas nora tapa milu/pra hiƞ apagawe sawa-neḥ saṅƞ awiku hakwe silib. riṅ laku kaki, hawis putuśe wirasa, pamantĕsiṅ wuwus hadikara maƞa/n sukla, tan len kaṅ densudya śuka wiṙyya śugiḥ hamriḥ polihi brata
    ø hana saragaƞel aƞliḥ kapa madiginĕṅ nitwasa, ha/mriḥ śukaniṅ pamukten. teku tapa walaƞun., gĕṅniṅ tamaḥ kaṅ denulati haƞurip urip driya, niṅ jabuṅ kasilib. hamet./ wrusaḥ riṅ laku lamon tan. wruḥ paraniṅ sandi haƞaku gaƞgajaran.
    ø tan makana sadyaniṅƞ akikin. saṅƞ amaƞgiḥ jatwani/ wacana, niṙ taṅ śuka lwan pamukten hupaṛga linbuṙ kalaniṅ pawestra lwiḥ kaṅ suṙggani wiṙyyawan niṙ tan tṛsna lampus paƞimuṙniṅ tala/na, datan aƞel bapa, lkasiṅ ƞalampahi prihĕn rasa menaka
    ø siƞamadya ṛƞĕ tutuṙ mami riṅƞ anmu rasa haja wiha/ natana śabda mule hatapa dentumuluś manawaṙṣa muliḥ hamukti saṅ wiku yen atatas. tan ulahianipun. manawa
    Folio 5vlipuṙ mmanaḥta,     budi lupa mawa kaṙyya cipta karasmi haṙsa waluyeƞ ampaḥ
    ø aneṅ kuna hanunuƞgal sakti hatwanta kawa/sā lumĕkas aƞummaduṙmma natareṅ sita prabatā dennatut daṙpan denya maƞun kasaktin kaśṛl winoṙr iṅ wig̈na, hyaṅƞ anaƞga/ ƞimuṙ śidḍa pinalih ajñana, śalaḥ sinpaṅ ciptane winoṙr iṅƞ asiḥ manasaṙ mareṅƞ ala
    ø datan kawaśana kṙti/ budi hanugal. jñana mariƞ ala wyaṙ ta tutuṙ/ tanpa gawe sṙṅniṅ lulut ṣumaput pamaṅcanani rara sakti hawali mariƞ ampaḥ keśaḥ kapalayu punika mewĕḥhi brata hiƞĕtiƞĕt./ siƞamaḋa hayo lali den.wruḥ kala rowaṅ
    ø lampaḥ halanak mami kapukaraṅ deni kṛtiṣamaya ṣarira yen duruṅƞa ka/puƞaṅ tmu haja hanacad. ṛgĕpiƞ ati hapan. wtuni dyata maṅkoliḥya tutuṙ tan. koniƞa maniṅƞ ulaḥ saṅ prasida tuhun i widya lampa/hi buḋi ka lan.
    ø waspada petaṅ haja tiniru ...i u goman iṅ daraḥ yyakya ñoloṅ baṣarane saṅ hyaṅƞ agama putus na/tarira samaḥ kakin. jñana depunatuwa ṛgĕp ka pamutus mapan wu pratameṅ raṣa dulurana kṛti jatmikaja silib. pet ṣaraṣani taya
    ø si/ƞamaḋa gaṙjita/ ḥiƞ ati manampani wƞaniki syara wira pta mirage maṅkya maṅgiḥ pamuwus. tutuṙ lwiḥ mawaraḥ yukti ṣabda paṅruwat mala, siƞamada mu
    Folio 5vwus     paƞeran tulusakna dera waraḥ kacaṙyyan rasaniƞ ati manira nuta lampaḥ
    ø yen ṣirameta luhuṙri wukiṙ nora kapaṅgiḥ jatini sabda/ tapa boƞoḥ/ kaky arane hawis kaṅ wruḥeṅ laku jumnĕƞa saṅ wruḥ gati sa tapa maƞadiya tan kabteṅ wuwus. mewĕḥ kaṅ jati wikana nadyan hudakṣinaha, denipunkari ta/n amagiḥya lampaḥ
    ø lwiḥ hutama ni ta saṅ wruḥ pamutusi tapa di ta pranaḥha hiya paṇḍi... rane nora bawa sa ṛsi muliḥ tutuṙ walaka, me tan aƞe/l kasni tapa sira saṅƞ amriḥ kasidan hakumanduṙma lawaṙ brata niṙ kabeḥ śenaka muṙwwa kitri jati pralina tan..... stu glare
    ø ƞ kaliƞane wuwusisun kaki ha/wis tuhuniṅƞ amaƞun tapa hakeḥ wi u paparanten kalawisaya ginuṅ kanuragan kaṅ denulati hawis amriḥya sunya ƞhi kawiṙyyan denguṅ haƞukiḥ daṙma kala/ḃan mayogama samady amriḥ wiji kitri daṙma kasukawakyan.
    ø tuhu panutuni hyaṅ hamṛdi ki paƞuwusan adan awaraḥ sawƞi tan ana g_liṅ ki siƞa/maḋa muwus ranakira haja winaraḥ jati haywage kumaliƞa, saṅ wani pamuwus. mewĕḥ kaṅ jaty awaraha twasniṅ rasa maṣa wuruƞa kapagiḥ, lamo/n kṛtasamaya
    ø /waniḥ saṅ wruḥ wiwaraniƞ aji tinaḋa glari maha ...dma hp iya hiku ḍapure patipatitisapun ṣaṅ winaṙṇa rakuti kawi pupuśe kumalama_ te
    Folio 6r maṅkin tan wruḥ     hawis bapa kaṅ wikana saṅƞ atapa ri sukma jñana wirati wruḥ panugali sabda
    ø prasidakna lampaḥta kaki huṅsinĕn ṣira saṅ yogi/syara sa mahapu/ruṣa ḍapure hana pamitranisun haṅlampaḥhi munidra lwiḥ makadini prawata kaṅ miṇaka guru liṅganiƞ adi patapan ṣukla pawitra w..ku/ brahmanacari jajaka hudakṣina
    ø sakti wiseśapra ri brata lwiḥ ka pika rohitani tapa sḍĕṅ tilasĕniƞ akweḥ haƞi tanakisun den./punbakti hatapa waṅsit ṣilakrama den.kna hulat den ..u u ul mewĕḥ riṅƞ amet nugraha kula hila bapa riṅƞ amat kadadin haƞel. raga/ nastapa
    ø pri waṅsitira saṅ daṙmajati petĕn ṣarasaniƞ adidrawa kombala g̈ni hurube ta na sumarupa tan katuduḥ kuruƞan mas niṙ tanpa cantri/ pakuk. wtuni tiga kabuyutan ṣuwuṅ kuwoṅ muni riƞ ambara takonakĕn ṣiƞamada hayo lali wkasiṅ paḍaṅƞ awa

    ø abyatni manaḥ kaluntuṙ pan lagya/ muƞakĕn waṅsi tan wruḥ glaṙ ñumananiḥ rag̈asamaya liƞipun manira nora kawasa, ṣarira gupe haƞliḥ tan wriṅ maṙgananisun laḥ yayi kariya sakti
    ø lṗas datan ana ketuṅ lamṗaḥhira saƞ anta/ li tlas prasinda lakune kadukaparani laku tan ana ni saṙga kakawaḥ luputi rahina wƞi niṙ sunya paranipun jñamut datan. kneƞ asṭi
    ø bina taṅ sunya piṗitu lamṗaḥe saṅ siḋa jati sukma taya tan ṗa/rane niṙmala taya kapukuṙ ri sunya taya kahaṙsa, ri sunya jati kaperi, tlas ṗarani laku ḋatan. kna ƞucap maniṅ

    ø hnĕƞakna rumuhun rag̈asamaya gĕ brati samṗun ṣumiwi bature saṅ pra/siḋa kṛta hayu, hana/ gantyani wawasawacana wuwus ni tejasari hagĕṅ brata laṅ ruƞu kasie tan lyan kahisṭi
    ø aƞṛƞĕ pasraniṅ wuwus ki surajaya, wus lalis riṅ pramriḥhan ibaṅ kilen pranaḥe masiḥ palaku
    Folio 75r ni tejasari hahmihaṙsa     luḥnya ḋṛs tumibeṅ pipi sasambatira mrasṣ ayun aƞatiya yen ṣira hasiḥ
    ø mugaḥ ri paturonipun kajaṅ siraḥ denṣukĕmi luḥ mijil adṛs tan pĕ/ten tibrani lara sa/gunuṅ polaḥe saśaya ketuṅ tan ṣipi laraniṅƞ ati hamiweka ti tñuḥ ni cipta maṙga ni pati
